# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Overview

**Task ID**: c_blockchain_nft_expert_071_architectural_understanding_expert_01
**Category**: architectural_understanding
**Difficulty**: expert
**Language**: c
**Context Length**: 1092663 tokens
**Files**: 84

## Task Title

Architectural Bottleneck Analysis for NFT Minting Throughput

## Description

HoloCanvas is experiencing significant user growth. During peak periods, especially when the 'Muse Observer' service triggers a system-wide 'evolution event' for the generative art, users report major delays. A minting operation, from user confirmation to the artifact appearing in the gallery, can take several minutes instead of seconds. This latency threatens user experience and platform stability. As a senior systems architect, your task is to analyze the current architecture, identify the primary performance bottleneck in the minting lifecycle, and propose a high-level architectural change to improve throughput and reduce latency under heavy load.

## Your Task

1. **Analyze and document the end-to-end data flow** for a new generative artifact (NFT) being minted and subsequently appearing in the `gallery_gateway`. Your analysis must trace the request across the relevant microservices, starting from the user interaction and ending with the data being queryable. Refer to the provided source code, especially the inter-service communication mechanisms.
2. **Identify the most likely architectural bottleneck** in this flow that would cause the described latency during a high-volume minting event. Justify your choice with evidence from the system's design (e.g., synchronous vs. asynchronous processing, on-chain vs. off-chain computation, data consistency models).
3. **Propose a specific, high-level architectural modification** to alleviate this bottleneck. Your proposal should not be a minor code fix but a change in how the services interact. Describe the new data flow and justify your design by explaining the trade-offs (e.g., in terms of complexity, cost, or data consistency).
4. **List the key files and the primary components/functions** within them that would need to be modified to implement your proposed solution. You do not need to write the code, only identify the modification points.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would approach this by first establishing a clear picture of the system's structure and data flow before attempting to diagnose the problem.

1.  **Initial Reconnaissance:** The developer would start by reading `ARCHITECTURE.md` to understand the high-level responsibilities of each microservice (`ledger_core`, `mint_factory`, `gallery_gateway`, etc.). The presence of `shared/kafka_client` and `shared/protocol/holocanvas.proto` is a critical clue that inter-service communication is asynchronous and event-driven via Kafka using Protocol Buffers.

2.  **Trace the Minting Flow:**
    *   A user request likely enters through the `wallet_proxy` and is forwarded to the `gallery_gateway`'s API (`api_handler.c`).
    *   The `gallery_gateway` constructs a formal transaction and submits it to the `ledger_core` for inclusion in the blockchain.
    *   `ledger_core`'s `transaction_processor.c` validates the transaction. The `block_builder.c` includes it in a new block, which is then finalized by the consensus mechanism (`consensus_manager.c` which likely uses one of the strategies like `pos_strategy.c`). This on-chain finalization is a synchronous, blocking step for each transaction.
    *   Upon block finalization, `ledger_core` (likely in `state_machine.c` or the consensus manager) emits a `BlockFinalized` or `TransactionConfirmed` event to a Kafka topic.
    *   `mint_factory`'s `event_handler.c` consumes this event from Kafka.
    *   Upon receiving the confirmation, it triggers the generative art logic in `recipe_composer.c` and `artifact_factory.c`. This is a computationally intensive step.
    *   Once the artifact is generated, `mint_factory` emits an `ArtifactCreated` event to another Kafka topic.
    *   `gallery_gateway`'s `query_service.c` consumes this `ArtifactCreated` event to update its internal, query-optimized cache/database, making the new artifact visible to users.

3.  **Diagnose the Bottleneck:** The developer would identify that processing each mint as a separate, unique on-chain transaction that must be fully finalized before the next step can begin is a classic scalability bottleneck. The `ledger_core` can only process a limited number of transactions per block/second. During a minting rush, a massive queue of transactions forms, waiting to be processed serially by the consensus mechanism. The computationally expensive generation process in `mint_factory` could also be a secondary bottleneck if it blocks the Kafka consumer from processing subsequent mint events.

4.  **Formulate a Solution:** The standard architectural pattern to solve this is to move from a one-by-one transactional model to a batch-processing or rollup-style model for minting.
    *   The proposal would involve creating a high-throughput, off-chain queue for mint requests (e.g., a new Kafka topic: `mint-intents`).
    *   A new or modified service (`batch_aggregator` component, possibly within `ledger_core` or as a standalone service) would consume from this queue, aggregate hundreds of mint requests into a single batch, and commit only the Merkle root of this batch to the main chain in a single transaction. This drastically reduces the load on the consensus mechanism.
    *   `mint_factory` would then listen for a `BatchConfirmed` event, retrieve the full batch data (e.g., from IPFS or a side-chain database, referenced in the on-chain transaction), and could then process the generation of all artifacts in the batch in parallel.

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Correct Flow Identification:** Accurately traces the minting data flow across at least `gallery_gateway`, `ledger_core`, and `mint_factory`, and correctly identifies Kafka as the communication bus.
- **Accurate Bottleneck Diagnosis:** Correctly identifies the on-chain, serial transaction processing in `ledger_core` as the primary scalability bottleneck.
- **Architectural Solution Viability:** Proposes a viable architectural solution, such as batching or a rollup mechanism, that fundamentally addresses the identified bottleneck.
- **Analysis of Trade-offs:** Discusses the trade-offs of the proposed solution, such as increased throughput at the cost of higher latency for individual mints and increased system complexity.
- **File-level Accuracy:** Correctly identifies the key services (`gallery_gateway`, `ledger_core`, `mint_factory`) and a plausible set of files within them that would require modification.
- **Use of Context:** Demonstrates understanding derived from file names and structure (e.g., `pos_strategy.c` implying pluggable consensus, `kafka_client` implying event-driven architecture) beyond just reading a single file's contents.

     1→/*
     2→ * HoloCanvas – Ledger Core
     3→ * File: block_builder.c
     4→ *
     5→ * Description:
     6→ *   The Block-Builder is responsible for assembling pending transactions into
     7→ *   candidate blocks and submitting them to the consensus engine for final
     8→ *   verification and commitment.  The module operates in its own worker thread,
     9→ *   watching the mem-pool for new transactions or a timeout, whichever comes
    10→ *   first.  Once triggered, it takes a consistent snapshot of the mem-pool,
    11→ *   builds a Merkle tree, computes the block header and forwards the block to
    12→ *   the Consensus service via gRPC.
    13→ *
    14→ *   The implementation favours robustness: it features extensive error
    15→ *   checking, clear separation between public and private API, and graceful
    16→ *   shutdown semantics.  All heap allocations are guarded, and the worker
    17→ *   thread is cancel-safe.
    18→ *
    19→ * Copyright (c) 2024, HoloCanvas Contributors
    20→ * SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT
    21→ */

     1→/*

     3→ *  File: query_service.c
     4→ *
     5→ *  Description:
     6→ *      The Query-Service is responsible for answering read-only requests
     7→ *      for NFT artifacts, gallery collections, and related metadata.  It
     8→ *      federates information from LedgerCore, Mint-Factory, and
     9→ *      Governance-Hall micro-services, while maintaining an in-process
    10→ *      LRU cache to alleviate hot-path latency.
    11→ *
    12→ *      This module purposefully contains _no_ outbound state-mutating
    13→ *      calls.  All updates are performed elsewhere in the platform.  The
    14→ *      service may be linked into a gRPC/REST transport layer (not
    15→ *      provided here) or embedded directly into another C component.
    16→ *
    17→ *  Build Dependencies:
    18→ *      - libcurl       (HTTP/gRPC over HTTP2 transport)
    19→ *      - cJSON         (Light-weight JSON DOM)
    20→ *      - uthash        (Single-header hash-table – https://troydhanson.github.io/uthash/)
    21→ *      - pthreads

    23→ *  Copyright:
    24→ *      MIT License – HoloCanvas Authors
    25→ */

43-assistanttext-
I have completed the architectural bottleneck analysis for the HoloCanvas NFT minting system. The solution document has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md`.

## Summary of Analysis

### 1. End-to-End Minting Flow
I traced the complete minting lifecycle through:
- **Wallet-Proxy** (`proxy_server.c`) - User entry point for transaction signing and broadcast
- **LedgerCore** - Transaction processing (`transaction_processor.c`), block building (`block_builder.c`), and consensus (`consensus_manager.c`)
- **Consensus Engine** - PoS strategy (`pos_strategy.c`) for block validation
- **Mint-Factory** - Event handling (`event_handler.c`) and artifact generation (`artifact_factory.c`, `recipe_composer.c`)
- **Gallery-Gateway** - Query service (`query_service.c`) for artifact retrieval

The services communicate via **Kafka** topics (configured in `kafka_topics.json`) and **gRPC** using Protocol Buffers (`holocanvas.proto`).

### 2. Primary Bottleneck Identified
**Serial, synchronous block processing in LedgerCore's consensus layer:**

1. The consensus manager (`consensus_manager.c:297-357`) processes blocks **one at a time** in a single worker thread
2. Transaction processor uses a **global mutex** (`transaction_processor.c:286-352`) for all state mutations
3. Each mint requires a full consensus round-trip before downstream services can proceed
4. The code explicitly acknowledges this: *"In production deployments we may employ sharded, fine-grained locks or MVCC to improve throughput."*

### 3. Proposed Solution: Batch Aggregation
A new **Batch Aggregator Service** that:
- Collects mint intents off-chain in a high-throughput Kafka queue
- Aggregates hundreds of mints into a single batch
- Commits only the Merkle root to the blockchain (one transaction instead of hundreds)
- E
... (truncated)

Design Patterns In-Use  \n8. Fault-Tolerance & Recovery  \n9. Deployment Topology  \n10. Appendix (Code Snippets, CLI, Make Targets)\n\n---\n\n## 1  Executive Summary\nHoloCanvas is an open, **C-based** micro-service ecosystem that orchestrates the minting, governance, and market evolution of **generative, living NFTs**. The system exposes deterministic *creative recipes* on-chain while delegating heavy media processing to off-chain worker pods. Each component is decoupled via **Kafka** event-streams and **gRPC** contracts, allowing horizontal scale-out and plug-and-play experimentation with consensus algorithms, artistic strategies, and DeFi mechanics.\n\n---\n\n## 2  High-Level Blueprint\n\n```text\n+------------------+        Kafka        +------------------+\n|  Wallet-Proxy    | <---- Topics ----> |  Gallery-Gateway |\n+--------+---------+                    +----+-------------+\n         |  gRPC HTTP /1.1                   |\n         |                                    |  Artifact REST\n         v                                    v\n +--------+---------+       +-----------------+-----------------+\n |  LedgerCore      | <---> |   Mint-Factory (Factory Pattern)  |\n +--------+---------+       +-----------------+-----------------+\n         |                                     ^\n         |  RocksDB (UTXO + State)             |  Event\n         v                                     |\n +--------+---------+       Kafka         +----+-------------+\n |  Governance-Hall | <---- Topics ---->  |  DeFi-Garden     |\n +------------------+                    +------------------+\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3  Component Reference\n\n### 3.1 Wallet-Proxy (Proxy Pattern)\n* Hides raw blockchain mechanics from UI clients.  \n* Signs and bundles transactions, batching micro-payments into rollups.  \n* Rate-limits requests per API key (Leaky-Bucket, per-tenant).  \n\n### 3.2 Gallery-Gateway  \n* API layer (OpenAPI v3) that exposes queryable GraphQL interface.  \n* HTTP \u2192 gRPC translation, static file CDN for media layers.  \n\n### 3.3 Mint-Factory (Factory Pattern)  \n* Composes shader fragments, audio grains, and metadata into an `ArtifactRecipe`.  \n* Emits `ArtifactCreated` events; persists recipe to **IPFS** and CID to chain.  \n\n### 3.4 LedgerCore  \n* Custom UTxO\u2010style ledger written in C with **RocksDB** backing store.  \n* Pluggable Consensus Engine (see \u00a76).  \n* Provides `LedgerService` (gRPC) with the following RPCs:  \n  - `SubmitTx(Tx)`  \n  - `StreamBlocks(Height)`  \n  - `QueryState(Key)`  \n\n### 3.5 Governance-Hall  \n* DAO voting, quorum tracking, parameter upgrades.  \n* Runs embedded **SQLite** + **Raft** for internal persistence.  \n\n### 3.6 DeFi-Garden  \n* Yield farming, staking pools, and fractional ownership of high-value NFTs.  \n* Uses **libsecp256k1** for cryptographic ops.  \n\n### 3.7 Oracle-Bridge  \n* Bridges external data (weather, stock, sensor) into on-chain events.  \n* Provides `WeatherOracleService.Report(WeatherFrame)`  \n\n### 3.8 Muse Services (Observer Pattern)  \n* Stateless pods that watch event streams (`ArtifactLiked`, `AuctionEnded`, etc.)  \n* Trigger generative `Strategy` plug-ins that mutate media layers.\n\n---\n\n## 4  Event & Data Contracts\n\n### 4.1 Kafka Topics\n| Topic | Publisher | Subscriber(s) | Payload Avro Schema |\n|-------|-----------|---------------|---------------------|\n| `tx.submitted` | Wallet-Proxy | LedgerCore | `TxEnvelope` |\n| `artifact.created` | Mint-Factory | Gallery-Gateway, Muse-* | `ArtifactMeta` |\n| `gov.vote.cast` | Wallet-Proxy | Governance-Hall | `VoteCast` |\n| `defi.stake` | Wallet-Proxy | DeFi-Garden | `StakeEvent` |\n| `oracle.weather` | Oracle-Bridge | Muse-Weather | `WeatherFrame` |\n\n### 4.2 gRPC / Protobuf\n```proto\nsyntax = \"proto3\";\npackage holo.ledger.v1;\n\nmessage Tx {\n  bytes  tx_id      = 1;\n  bytes  sender     = 2;\n  bytes  recipient  = 3;\n  uint64 amount     = 4;\n  bytes  signature  = 5;\n}\n\nservice LedgerService {\n  rpc SubmitTx     (Tx)       returns (Ack);\n  rpc StreamBlocks (Height)   returns (stream Block);\n  rpc QueryState   (StateKey) returns (StateValue);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5  Life-Cycle State Machine\n\n```mermaid\nstateDiagram-v2\n    [*] --> Draft\n    Draft --> Curated : curator.approve()\n    Curated --> Auction : schedule.auction()\n    Auction --> Fractionalized : reserve.price.met()\n    Fractionalized --> Staked : defi.stake()\n    Staked --> Archived : life.span.expired()\n```\n\nStates are enforced inside **LedgerCore** by a compiled **deterministic automaton** defined in `state_machine.c` (see Appendix).\n\n---\n\n## 6  Consensus Engine Plug-In Model\n\n`LedgerCore` dynamically loads shared-object libraries at runtime:\n\n```c\ntypedef struct {\n    const char  *name;\n    int  (*init)(void);\n    int  (*validate_block)(const block_t *);\n    int  (*commit)(const block_t *);\n    void (*shutdown)(void);\n} consensus_vtable_t;\n```\n\n1. `libconsensus_pos.so` \u2013 traditional Proof-of-Stake.  \n2. `libconsensus_da.so`  \u2013 Delegated-Artistry (weighted by curation reputation).  \n\nEach plug-in must export a `consensus_vtable` symbol.\n\n---\n\n## 7  Design Patterns In-Use\n* **Factory** \u2013 `Mint-Factory` building artifacts.  \n* **Observer** \u2013 Muse services listening to events.  \n* **Strategy** \u2013 Generation strategies loaded by Muse pods.  \n* **Proxy** \u2013 Wallet-Proxy shielding clients.  \n* **State Machine** \u2013 Artifact life-cycle.  \n* **Event Driven** \u2013 Kafka message bus.\n\n---\n\n## 8  Fault-Tolerance & Recovery\n1. **At-Least-Once** event semantics; idempotent consumers use `dedupe_key`.  \n2. **Circuit Breakers** guard cross-service gRPC calls.  \n3. **Checksum** of every CID before pinning to IPFS & chain.  \n4. **Snapshotting** Ledger state each 1000 blocks; restores via **RocksDB checkpoint API**.  \n5. **Draining Mode**: Kubernetes preStop hook flushes pending tx to `tx.submitted`.\n\n---\n\n## 9  Deployment Topology\n\n```text\n                       \"Missing or invalid fields\");\n    }\n\n    if (!validate_uuid(artifact_id)) {\n        json_decref(root);\n        return http_text_reply(connection, RESP_BAD_REQUEST,\n                               \"Invalid artifact_id\");\n    }\n\n    uint64_t amount = 0;\n    if (json_is_integer(amount_node)) {\n        amount = (uint64_t)json_integer_value(amount_node);\n    } else { status_code,\n                json_t *body)\n{\n    char *dump = json_dumps(body, JSON_INDENT | JSON_ENSURE_ASCII);\n    struct MHD_Response *resp = MHD_create_response_from_buffer(\n        strlen(dump), (void *)dump, MHD_RESPMEM_MUST_FREE);\n    if (!resp) { free(dump); return MHD_NO; }\n\n    MHD_add_response_header(resp, \"Content-Type\", \"application/json\");\n    int ret = tp_process(txp_ctx_t *ctx, const uint8_t *raw, size_t raw_len)\n{\n    if (!ctx || !raw || !raw_len) {\n        return -EINVAL;\n    }\n\n    /* Decode/deserialize */\n    tx_t tx;\n    memset(&tx, 0,     pthread_mutex_unlock(&ctx->mtx);\n        return 2; /* nonce mismatch */\n    }\n    if (!tp_verify_funds(ctx, &tx)) {\n        pthread_mutex_lock(&ctx->mtx);\n        ctx->stats.rejected_balance++;\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&ctx->mtx);\n        return 3; /* insufficient funds */\n    }\n\n    /* \u2500\u2500 Critical section: apply & emit event \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n    if (tp_apply(ctx, */\n\n/*\n * Signature verification\n */\nstatic bool tp_verify_signature(const tx_t *tx)\n{\n    if (!tx) return false;\n\n    /* Ed25519 public key & signature size are fixed (32 / 64 bytes) */\n    if (tx->sig_len != 64 || tx->pubkey_len != 32) {\n        log_debug(\"tp_verify_signature: malformed key/sig\");\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* Hash the canonicalised, signature-free frame of the transaction */\n    uint8_t digest[32];\n    if (sha3_256(tx->frame, tx->frame_len, digest) != 0) {\n        log_error(\"tp_verify_signature: sha3_256 failed\");\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    const bool ok = ed25519_verify(tx->signature, digest, sizeof(digest),\n                                   tx->pubkey);\n    if (!ok) {\n        log_debug(\"tp_verify_signature: invalid signature for tx %s\", tx->tx_id);\n    }\n    return ok;\n}\n\n/*\n * Nonce verification\n *   Protects against replay and preserves causal order per-account.\n */\nstatic bool tp_verify_nonce(txp_ctx_t *ctx, const tx_t *tx)\n{\n    account_state_t acct;\n    if (ledger_get_account_state(ctx->ledger, tx->from, &acct) != 0) {\n        log_debug(\"tp_verify_nonce: unknown account %s\", tx->from);\n        return false; /* account must exist */\n    }\n\n    const bool ok = (tx->nonce == acct.next_nonce);\n    if (!ok) {\n        log_debug(\"tp_verify_nonce: expected nonce=%\" PRIu64 \", got=%\" PRIu64,\n                  acct.next_nonce, tx->nonce);\n    }\n    return ok;\n}\n\n/*\n * Balance / funds verification\n */\nstatic bool tp_verify_funds(txp_ctx_t *ctx, const tx_t *tx)\n{\n    account_state_t acct;\n    if (ledger_get_account_state(ctx->ledger, tx->from, &acct) != 0) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* Gas cost: base + payload-dependent */\n    const uint64_t gas_cost = tx->gas_price * tx->gas_limit;\n    const uint64_t total    = gas_cost + tx->value;\n\n    const bool ok = (acct.balance >= total);\n    if (!ok) {\n        log_debug(\"tp_verify_funds: balance %\" */\n\n/*\n * tp_apply()\n *   Mutate ledger state and any domain-level state-machines.\n *\n *   NOTE: called inside the global mutex for now.  In production deployments\n *   we may employ sharded, fine-grained locks or MVCC to improve throughput.\n */\nstatic int tp_apply(txp_ctx_t *ctx, const tx_t *tx, uint64_t ts_unix)\n{\n    int rc = 0;\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&ctx->mtx);\n\n    /* Append ledger entry \u2013 durable write-ahead log (WAL) */\n    ledger_entry_t entry = {\n        .timestamp  = ts_unix,\n        .tx_id      = {0},\n        .raw        = tx->raw,\n        .raw_len    = tx->raw_len\n    };\n    memcpy(entry.tx_id, tx->tx_id, sizeof(entry.tx_id));\n\n    if ((rc = ledger_append(ctx->ledger, &entry)) != 0) {\n        log_error(\"tp_apply: ledger_append failed (rc=%d)\", rc);\n        goto exit;\n    }\n\n    /* Update account nonce & balance */\n    if ((rc = ledger_inc_nonce(ctx->ledger, tx->from)) != 0) {\n        log_error(\"tp_apply: ledger_inc_nonce failed\");\n        goto exit;\n    }\n    if ((rc = ledger_debit(ctx->ledger, tx->from,\n                           tx->value + (tx->gas_price * tx->gas_limit))) != 0) {\n        log_error(\"tp_apply: ledger_debit failed\");\n        goto exit;\n    }\n    if (tx->value > 0 && tx->to[0] != '\\0') {\n        if ((rc = ledger_credit(ctx->ledger, tx->to, tx->value)) != 0) {\n            log_error(\"tp_apply: ledger_credit failed\");\n            goto exit;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /* Domain-specific: NFT state transitions, governance votes, etc. */\n    switch (tx->type) {\n        case TX_MINT_NFT:\n            rc = artifact_state_on_mint(ctx->ledger, &tx->payload.mint);\n            break;\n        case TX_TRANSFER_NFT:\n            rc = artifact_state_on_transfer(ctx->ledger, &tx->payload.transfer);\n            break;\n        case TX_GOVERNANCE_VOTE:\n            rc = governance_apply_vote(ctx->ledger, &tx->payload.vote);\n            break;\n        case TX_STATE_MACHINE_EVOLUTION:\n            rc = artifact_state_transition(ctx->ledger, &tx->payload.evolve);\n            break;\n        default:\n            /* For payment-only transactions nothing else to do */\n            break;\n    }\n\n    if (rc != 0) {\n        log_error(\"tp_apply: domain mutation failed (rc=%d)\", rc);\n        /* TODO: roll-back ledger_write via undo-log once implemented */\n    }\n\nexit:\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&ctx->mtx);\n    return rc;\n}\n\n/* */\n/*---------------------------------------------------------------------------*/\n\n/**\n * Basic heuristic validation of recipe fragments.\n * In production this would call out to a sandboxed                              cJSON_CreateString(fr->metadata ? fr->metadata : \"\"));\n    }\n\n    return root;\n}\n\n/**\n * Compute SHA-256 digest and return as lowercase hex string.\n */\nstatic    consuming protobuf / JSON events on the project-wide Event Bus.\n *\n *  Design notes:\n *      \u2022 One producer instance and one consumer instance are multiplexed out of\n *        a single caller\u2019s thread.\n *      \u2022 Delivery reports are routed to a ring-buffer so that infrequent callers\n *        can inspect them without registering a full callback.\n *      \u2022 All public API symbols are prefixed with \u201chc_kafka_\u201d.\n *\n *  Build:\n *      gcc -Wall -Wextra -pedantic -std=c11 \\\n *          -I/path/to/librdkafka/include -L/path/to/librdkafka/lib \\\n *          -lrdkafka -pthread -o hc_kafka.o -c hc_kafka.c\n */\n\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include <stdarg.h>\n#include <signal.h>\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <errno.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n#include <librdkafka/rdkafka.h>\n\n#include \"hc_kafka.h\"   /* Public header exported to the rest of the project    */\n\n/* \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n/*                           Compile-time Defaults                           */\n\n#ifndef HC_KAFKA_LOG_PREFIX\n#   define HC_KAFKA_LOG_PREFIX  \"[hc_kafka] \"\n#endif\n\n#ifndef */\n/*                                 Logging                                   */\n\nstatic void hc_kafka_vlog(enum hc_kafka_log_level lvl,\n                          const char *fmt, va_list vfprintf(stream, fmt, ap);\n    fprintf(stream, \"\\n\");\n    funlockfile(stream);\n}\n\nstatic void hc_kafka_log(enum hc_kafka_log_level lvl, const char *fmt, ...)\n{\n    va_list ap;\n    mutex;\n} delivery_ring_t;\n\nstatic void ring_init(delivery_ring_t *r)\n{\n    memset(r, 0, sizeof(*r));\n    pthread_mutex_init(&r->mutex, NULL);\n}\n\nstatic void ring_push(delivery_ring_t *r, const hc_kafka_delivery_t *item)\n{\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&r->mutex);\n    r->buf[r->head] = *item;\n    r->head = (r->head + 1) % HC_KAFKA_MAX_DELIVERY_RING;\n    if (r->head == r->tail) {          /* overwrite oldest */\n        r->tail = (r->tail + 1) % HC_KAFKA_MAX_DELIVERY_RING;\n    }\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&r->mutex);\n}\n\nstatic int ring_pop(delivery_ring_t *r, hc_kafka_delivery_t *out)\n{\n    int found = 0;\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&r->mutex);\n    if (r->tail != r->head) {\n        *out = r->buf[r->tail];\n        r->tail = (r->tail + 1) % HC_KAFKA_MAX_DELIVERY_RING;\n  enum hc_kafka_log_level lvl;\n\n    /* Map librdkafka logs to our own */\n    if (level >= 6)\n        lvl = HC_KAFKA_LOG_DEBUG;\n    else if (level >= 4)\n        lvl = HC_KAFKA_LOG_INFO;\n    else\n        lvl = HC_KAFKA_LOG_WARN;\n\n    hc_kafka_log(lvl, \"rdkafka: %s\", buf);\n}\n\nstatic void dr_msg_cb(rd_kafka_t *rk,\n                      const rd_kafka_message_t *m,\n                      void *opaque)\n{\n    hc_kafka_client_t *cli = (hc_kafka_client_t *)opaque;\n    hc_kafka_delivery_t d  = {\n        .topic      = m->rkt ? rd_kafka_topic_name(m->rkt) : NULL,\n        .partition All micro-services\u2014Cryptograph,\n//      LedgerCore, MintFactory, GalleryGateway, DeFiGarden, OracleBridge,\n//      WalletProxy, and GovernanceHall\u2014share this file to guarantee binary\n//      compatibility across language stacks (C, Go, Rust, TS, \u2026).\n//\n//      The protocol is designed for high-throughput event streaming while still\n//      allowing fine-grained, request/response RPCs where appropriate.\n//      Multiplexed topic identifiers (topic_id) let a single bidirectional\n//      stream carry heterogeneous event types without sacrificing strong type\n//      safety.\n//\n//  Notes:\n//      1. All domain objects include an immutable uuid and a RFC-3339 timestamp.\n//      2. Blockchain \u201cblock_height\u201d indexes finalized state on the roll-up\n//         layer.  A value of 0 means \u201cpending / mem-pool\u201d.                 ]:-)\n//\n//  Copyright \u00a9 2023-2024 The HoloCanvas Authors.\n//\n\npackage holocanvas.v1;\n\noption csharp_namespace  = \"HoloCanvas.Proto\";\noption java_package      = \"com.holocanvas.proto.v1\";\noption go_package        = \"github.com/holocanvas/proto/gen/go/holocanvas/v1;holocanvasv1\";\noption objc_class_prefix = \"HCX\";\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Google Well-Known Types\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nimport \"google/protobuf/any.proto\";\nimport \"google/protobuf/struct.proto\";\nimport \"google/protobuf/timestamp.proto\";\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// ENUMERATIONS\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nenum ArtifactState {\n    ARTIFACT_STATE_UNSPECIFIED  = 0;\n    ARTIFACT_STATE_DRAFT        = 1;\n    ARTIFACT_STATE_CURATED      = 2;\n    ARTIFACT_STATE_AUCTION      = 3;\n    ARTIFACT_STATE_FRACTIONAL   = 4;\n    ARTIFACT_STATE_STAKED       = 5;\n    ARTIFACT_STATE_ARCHIVED     = 6;\n}\n\nenum MediaKind {\n    MEDIA_KIND_UNSPECIFIED = 0;\n    MEDIA_KIND_SHADER      = 1;   // GLSL / WGSL fragment\n    MEDIA_KIND_AUDIO       = 2;   // WebAudio / MIDI\n    MEDIA_KIND_METADATA    = 3;   // JSON-LD, IPFS CID, etc.\n}\n\nenum GovernanceAction {\n    GOVERNANCE_ACTION_UNSPECIFIED = 0;\n    GOVERNANCE_ACTION_MINT_RIGHTS = 1;\n    GOVERNANCE_ACTION_CURATE      = 2;\n    GOVERNANCE_ACTION_EVOLVE      = 3;\n    GOVERNANCE_ACTION_FREEZE      = 4;\n    GOVERNANCE_ACTION_BURN        = 5;\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// CORE DOMAIN OBJECTS\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n// A cryptographically provable identity (wallet, service, or DAO).\nmessage Principal {\n    string  did           = 1;  // W3C Decentralized Identifier, e.g. \"did:key:\u2026\"\n    bytes   public_key    = 2;  // Raw secp256k1 key bytes\n    string  alias         = 3;  // Human-friendly label\n}\n\n// Represents a single layer of media inside an Artifact.\nmessage MediaLayer {\n    string      uuid            = 1;  // Layer UUID\n    MediaKind   kind            = 2;\n    string      content_uri     = 3;  // IPFS / Arweave / HTTPS URI\n    bytes       content_hash    = 4;  // SHA-256 digest of raw bytes\n    uint32      ordinal         = 5;  // Z-index for compositing\n    google.protobuf.Timestamp created_at = 6;\n}\n\n// Immutable recipe captured at mint-time.\nmessage ArtifactRecipe {\n    string                        uuid          = 1;\n    repeated MediaLayer           layers        = 2;\n    google.protobuf.Struct        metadata      = 3;  // Arbitrary creator-supplied JSON\n    string                        factory_addr  = 4;  // On-chain smart-contract address\n    google.protobuf.Timestamp     created_at    = 5;\n}\n\n// NFT Artifact tracked on-chain.\nmessage Artifact {\n    string               uuid           = 1;\n    ArtifactState        state          = 2;\n    ArtifactRecipe       recipe         = 3;\n    Principal            owner          = 4;\n    uint64               block_height   = 5;  // 0 => pending\n    google.protobuf.Timestamp updated_at = 6;\n}\n\n// Generic financial amount in Wei, USD-cents, etc.\nmessage Amount {\n    string  currency = 1; // e.g. \"wei\", \"usdc\"\n    uint64  value    = 2;\n}\n\n// Bid placed during Auction state.\nmessage Bid {\n    string                   uuid         = 1;\n    string                   artifact_uuid= 2;\n    Principal                bidder       = 3;\n    Amount                   amount       = 4;\n    google.protobuf.Timestamp placed_at   = 5;\n}\n\n// Staking position.\nmessage Stake {\n    string                   uuid          = 1;\n    string                   artifact_uuid = 2;\n    Principal                staker        = 3;\n    Amount                   amount        = 4;\n    uint32                   lock_days     = 5;\n    google.protobuf.Timestamp staked_at    = 6;\n}\n\n// Governance proposal document.\nmessage GovernanceProposal {\n    string                       uuid            = 1;\n    string                       artifact_uuid   = 2;\n    GovernanceAction             action          = 3;\n    google.protobuf.Struct       params          = 4;  // action-specific\n    Principal                    proposer        = 5;\n    google.protobuf.Timestamp    submitted_at    = 6;\n    repeated GovernanceVote      votes           = 7;\n}\n\n// Individual vote.\nmessage GovernanceVote {\n    Principal                    voter        = 1;\n    bool                         approve      = 2;\n    google.protobuf.Timestamp    cast_at      = 3;\n}\n\n// Data injected by external oracle feeds.\nmessage OracleEvent {\n    string                       uuid          = 1;\n    string                       source        = 2; // e.g. \"openweather\"\n    google.protobuf.Struct       payload       = 3;\n    google.protobuf.Timestamp    observed_at   = 4;\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// TRANSACTION ENVELOPE\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n// Unified event wrapper for streaming across Kafka / gRPC.\nmessage CanvasEvent {\n    string   uuid        = 1;\n    oneof    body {\n        Artifact            artifact              = 10;\n        Bid                 bid                   = 11;\n        Stake               stake                 = 12;\n        GovernanceProposal  proposal              = 13;\n        OracleEvent         oracle                = 14;\n    }\n    // Topic to aid in routing through pub/sub fabric.\n    string   topic_id    = 20; // e.g. \"artifact.{uuid}\" or \"governance.global\"\n    uint64   block_height= 21;\n    google.protobuf.Timestamp emitted_at = 22;\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// SERVICE APIs\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n// 1. Factory Pattern \u2013 composable mint pipeline.\nservice MintFactory {\n    // Mint a brand-new Artifact from a recipe.\n    rpc Mint(ArtifactRecipe) returns (Artifact);\n\n    // Retrieve an existing Artifact (regardless of state).\n    rpc GetArtifact(GetArtifactRequest) returns (Artifact);\n\n    // Subscribe to live state transitions for a specific Artifact.\n    rpc WatchArtifact(WatchArtifactRequest) returns (stream CanvasEvent);\n}\n\nmessage GetArtifactRequest {\n    string artifact_uuid = 1;\n}\n\nmessage WatchArtifactRequest {\n    string artifact_uuid = 1;\n}\n\n// 2. LedgerCore \u2013 canonical blockchain interface (light wrapper around rollup node).\nservice LedgerCore {\n    // Append a signed transaction to the roll-up mem-pool.\n    rpc SubmitEvent(CanvasEvent) returns (SubmitEventResponse);\n\n    // Stream finalized blocks for indexing or archival.\n    rpc StreamBlocks(StreamBlocksRequest) returns (stream CanvasEvent);\n}\n\nmessage SubmitEventResponse {\n    string  tx_hash      = 1;\n    uint64  mempool_seq  = 2;\n}\n\nmessage StreamBlocksRequest {\n    uint64 from_block = 1;\n}\n\n// 3. DeFiGarden \u2013 staking & fractionalization hub.\nservice DeFiGarden {\n    rpc StakeArtifact(Stake) returns (Stake);\n    rpc Unstake(UnstakeRequest) returns (Stake);\n    rpc WatchStakes(WatchStakesRequest) returns (stream Stake);\n}\n\nmessage UnstakeRequest {\n    string stake_uuid = 1;\n}\n\nmessage WatchStakesRequest {\n    string artifact_uuid = 1;\n}\n\n// 4. GovernanceHall \u2013 DAO governance portal.\nservice GovernanceHall {\n    rpc Propose(GovernanceProposal) returns (GovernanceProposal);\n    rpc Vote(GovernanceVote) returns (GovernanceProposal);\n    rpc WatchGovernance(WatchGovernanceRequest) returns (stream GovernanceProposal);\n}\n\nmessage WatchGovernanceRequest {\n    string artifact_uuid = 1; // empty = global stream\n}\n\n// 5. OracleBridge \u2013 gateway for external data feeds.\nservice OracleBridge {\n    rpc InjectOracleData(OracleEvent) returns (OracleEvent);\n    rpc WatchOracle(WatchOracleRequest) returns (stream OracleEvent);\n}\n\nmessage WatchOracleRequest {\n    string source = 1; // empty = all\n}\n\n// 6. WalletProxy \u2013 abstraction layer for user wallets.\nservice WalletProxy {\n    rpc SignAndSubmit(SignedPayload) returns (SubmitEventResponse);\n    rpc GetBalance(GetBalanceRequest) returns (Amount);\n}\n\nmessage SignedPayload {\n    bytes  payload   = 1;\n    bytes  signature = 2;\n}\n\nmessage GetBalanceRequest {\n    Principal account = 1;\n}\n\n// 7. GalleryGateway \u2013 read-only aggregation for UI/REST.\nservice GalleryGateway {\n    rpc ListArtifacts(ListArtifactsRequest) returns (stream Artifact);\n}\n\nmessage ListArtifactsRequest {\n    ArtifactState state_filter = 1; // UNSPECIFIED = all\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// BACKWARD-COMPATIBILITY NOTES\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// \u2022 Whenever you need to remove a field, use the \u201creserved\u201d keyword to prevent\n//   accidental reuse.  (See Proto3 versioning guide.)\n// \u2022 Keep numeric tags stable once published.\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------",

    "content": "/*\n * HoloCanvas \u2013 LedgerCore\n * Proof-of-Stake Consensus Strategy\n *\n * File:    strategies/pos_strategy.c\n * Author:  HoloCanvas Core Team\n *\n * Description:\n *   This file implements the Proof-of-Stake (PoS) consensus plug-in for the\n *   LedgerCore micro-service.  The strategy is loaded at runtime through a\n *   Strategy-Pattern interface (see pos_strategy.h) and receives a stream of\n *   ledger events via the internal Event-Bus.  The PoS module is responsible\n *   for:\n *\n *     \u2022 Managing validator stake tables\n *     \u2022 Electing the next block proposer with a stake-weighted VRF\n *     \u2022 Verifying block signatures and stake lock-ups\n *     \u2022 Distributing block rewards and slashing misbehaving validators\n *\n *   The implementation is production-grade and is optimised for readability\n *   and robustness rather than raw performance.  Critical sections are\n *   protected by pthread mutexes; cryptographic operations rely on libsodium.\n *\n *   NOTE: The surrounding infrastructure (ledger storage, event bus, etc.)\n *         is mocked by forward declarations to keep this file self-contained.\n *         In the full code-base these come from their respective headers.\n *\n * License:\n *   Apache-2.0\n */\n\n#include <assert.h>\n#include <errno.h>\n#include <inttypes.h>\n#include <sodium.h>\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include \"pos_strategy.h\"  /* Public interface */\n#include \"../include/crypto_utils.h\"      /* crypto_sign_block(), hash(), \u2026 */\n#include \"../include/event_bus.h\"         /* event_bus_publish(), \u2026 */\n#include \"../include/ledger_storage.h\"    /* ledger_get_balance(), \u2026 */\n#include \"../include/logger.h\"            /* HC_LOG_DEBUG(), \u2026 */\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                              Local  Types                                 *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/* Validator entry kept in memory; periodically snapshotted to disk */\ntypedef struct validator_entry_s\n{\n    wallet_addr_t  address;        /* 32-byte public key (bech32-decoded) */\n    uint64_t       stake;          /* Currently bonded stake              */\n    uint64_t       locked_until;   /* Epoch height until which stake is locked */\n    uint64_t       rewards;        /* Pending rewards (lazy withdrawn)    */\n    bool           jailed;         /* true when validator is slashed      */\n} validator_entry_t;\n\n/* Main PoS context \u2013 one per service instance */\ntypedef struct pos_ctx_s\n{\n    validator_entry_t *validators; /* Dynamic array                       */\n    size_t             v_len;      /* Elements in the array               */\n    size_t             v_cap;      /* Capacity                            */\n\n    uint64_t           total_stake;/* Aggregate bonded stake              */\n    uint64_t           current_epoch;\n    event_bus_t       *bus;        /* Weak ref to global Event-Bus        */\n\n    pthread_rwlock_t   rwlock;     /* Protects validators & total_stake   */\n} pos_ctx_t;\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                       Forward Declarations / Helpers                      *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nstatic int      ensure_capacity(pos_ctx_t *ctx);\nstatic ssize_t  find_validator(pos_ctx_t *ctx, const wallet_addr_t addr);\nstatic int      add_validator(pos_ctx_t *ctx,\n                              const wallet_addr_t addr,\n                              uint64_t stake);\n\nstatic int      vrf_elect(const pos_ctx_t *ctx,\n                          const uint8_t previous_block_hash[crypto_hash_sha256_BYTES],\n                          wallet_addr_t out_selected);\n\nstatic int      apply_block_rewards(pos_ctx_t *ctx,\n                                    const wallet_addr_t proposer,\n                                    uint64_t block_fees);\n\nstatic int      slash_validator(pos_ctx_t *ctx,\n                                const wallet_addr_t address,\n                                const char *reason);\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                       Public  Interface  (Strategy)                       *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nstatic pos_ctx_t g_ctx;  /* Singleton instance \u2013 strategy is process-local */\n\n\n/*\n * pos_strategy_init()\n * -------------------\n * Initialise libsodium (if necessary), internal state and subscribe to the\n * Event-Bus streams required by the PoS module.\n */\nint\npos_strategy_init(event_bus_t *bus)\n{\n    if (sodium_init() == -1) {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"[PoS] libsodium init failed\\n\");\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    memset(&g_ctx, 0, sizeof(g_ctx));\n    g_ctx.bus = bus;\n    pthread_rwlock_init(&g_ctx.rwlock, NULL);\n\n    /* Pre-allocate validator table with a sane default */\n    g_ctx.v_cap = 64;\n    g_ctx.validators = calloc(g_ctx.v_cap, sizeof(validator_entry_t));\n    if (!g_ctx.validators) {\n        perror(\"[PoS] calloc validators\");\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    /* Subscribe to ledger events (mocked) */\n    event_bus_subscribe(bus, EVENT_STAKE_BOND,  pos_strategy_on_event);\n    event_bus_subscribe(bus, EVENT_STAKE_UNBOND,pos_strategy_on_event);\n    event_bus_subscribe(bus, EVENT_NEW_BLOCK,   pos_strategy_on_event);\n\n    HC_LOG_INFO(\"[PoS] strategy initialised\");\n    return 0;\n}\n\n\n/*\n * pos_strategy_shutdown()\n * -----------------------\n * Flush any in-memory state to durable storage and cleanup allocations.\n */\nvoid\npos_strategy_shutdown(void)\n{\n    pthread_rwlock_wrlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n\n    /* In a real implementation we would persist validator snapshots here */\n\n    free(g_ctx.validators);\n    g_ctx.validators = NULL;\n    g_ctx.v_len      = 0;\n    g_ctx.v_cap      = 0;\n    g_ctx.total_stake= 0;\n\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n    pthread_rwlock_destroy(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n\n    HC_LOG_INFO(\"[PoS] strategy shut down\");\n}\n\n\n/*\n * pos_strategy_on_event()\n * -----------------------\n * Central entry point for Event-Bus callbacks.  Handles three primary event\n * classes: stake bond/unbond, and new block arrival.\n */\nvoid\npos_strategy_on_event(const event_t *ev)\n{\n    switch (ev->type) {\n\n    case EVENT_STAKE_BOND:\n        pos_strategy_handle_bond((const stake_event_t *)ev->payload);\n        break;\n\n    case EVENT_STAKE_UNBOND:\n        pos_strategy_handle_unbond((const stake_event_t *)ev->payload);\n        break;\n\n    case EVENT_NEW_BLOCK:\n        pos_strategy_handle_block((const block_event_t *)ev->payload);\n        break;\n\n    default:\n        HC_LOG_WARN(\"[PoS] unknown event type: %d\", (int)ev->type);\n    }\n}\n\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                          Event  Handlers                                  *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/*\n * Handle stake bonding.  Updates validator table and total stake.\n */\nvoid\npos_strategy_handle_bond(const stake_event_t *ev)\n{\n    int rc;\n    pthread_rwlock_wrlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n\n    ssize_t idx = find_validator(&g_ctx, ev->staker);\n    if (idx < 0) {\n        /* New validator */\n        rc = add_validator(&g_ctx, ev->staker, ev->amount);\n        if (rc != 0) {\n            HC_LOG_ERROR(\"[PoS] failed to add validator\");\n            pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n            return;\n        }\n    } else {\n        validator_entry_t *v = &g_ctx.validators[idx];\n        v->stake += ev->amount;\n        v->locked_until = g_ctx.current_epoch + POS_MIN_LOCK_EPOCHS;\n    }\n\n    g_ctx.total_stake += ev->amount;\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n\n    HC_LOG_DEBUG(\"[PoS] bonded %\" PRIu64 \" to validator %.8s\u2026, total=%\" PRIu64,\n                 ev->amount, ev->staker, g_ctx.total_stake);\n}\n\n\n/*\n * Handle stake unbonding request.  Stake is not immediately released: we place\n * it in a cooldown queue (omitted for brevity) and unlock once the holding\n * period expires.\n */\nvoid\npos_strategy_handle_unbond(const stake_event_t *ev)\n{\n    pthread_rwlock_wrlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n\n    ssize_t idx = find_validator(&g_ctx, ev->staker);\n    if (idx < 0) {\n        HC_LOG_WARN(\"[PoS] unbond from unknown validator %.8s\u2026\", ev->staker);\n        pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n        return;\n    }\n\n    validator_entry_t *v = &g_ctx.validators[idx];\n    if (v->stake < ev->amount) {\n        HC_LOG_ERROR(\"[PoS] unbond exceeds stake\");\n        pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n        return;\n    }\n\n    v->stake -= ev->amount;\n    g_ctx.total_stake -= ev->amount;\n\n    /* TODO: Push to cooldown queue for delayed release */\n\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n\n    HC_LOG_DEBUG(\"[PoS] unbonded %\" PRIu64 \" from validator %.8s\u2026, remaining=%\"\n                 PRIu64, ev->amount, ev->staker, v->stake);\n}\n\n\n/*\n * Handle new block arrival.  Verify proposer signature and stake, distribute\n * fees and reward, then increment epoch if necessary.\n */\nvoid\npos_strategy_handle_block(const block_event_t *ev)\n{\n    const block_t *blk = &ev->block;\n\n    /* 1. Verify signature */\n    if (crypto_verify_block(blk) != 0) {\n        HC_LOG_ERROR(\"[PoS] invalid block signature\");\n        /* TODO: Reject block on the ledger pipeline */\n        return;\n    }\n\n    /* 2. Ensure proposer is valid and not jailed */\n    pthread_rwlock_rdlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n    ssize_t idx = find_validator(&g_ctx, blk->proposer);\n    if (idx < 0) {\n        pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n        HC_LOG_ERROR(\"[PoS] proposer %.8s\u2026 not in validator set\", blk->proposer);\n        return;\n    }\n\n    const validator_entry_t *v = &g_ctx.validators[idx];\n    if (v->jailed) {\n        pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n        HC_LOG_ERROR(\"[PoS] jailed proposer %.8s\u2026\", blk->proposer);\n        /* Slash attempt */\n        slash_validator(&g_ctx, blk->proposer, \"Proposed block while jailed\");\n        return;\n    }\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n\n    /* 3. Apply rewards */\n    if (apply_block_rewards(&g_ctx, blk->proposer, blk->fees) != 0) {\n        HC_LOG_ERROR(\"[PoS] reward distribution failed\");\n    }\n\n    /* 4. Advance epoch if block boundary crossed */\n    if (blk->height % POS_BLOCKS_PER_EPOCH == 0) {\n        g_ctx.current_epoch++;\n        HC_LOG_INFO(\"[PoS] epoch advanced to %\" PRIu64, g_ctx.current_epoch);\n    }\n}\n\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                    Consensus / Validator Selection                        *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/*\n * pos_strategy_select_proposer()\n * ------------------------------\n * Called by the block-production pipeline to pick the next validator who\n * is eligible to create a block.  Uses a VRF to achieve randomness that\n * can be independently verified by all peers.\n *\n * Returns 0 on success and fills `out_addr`.\n */\nint\npos_strategy_select_proposer(const uint8_t prev_block_hash[crypto_hash_sha256_BYTES],\n                             wallet_addr_t out_addr)\n{\n    pthread_rwlock_rdlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n    if (g_ctx.total_stake == 0 || g_ctx.v_len == 0) {\n        pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n        HC_LOG_ERROR(\"[PoS] no stake available for selection\");\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    int rc = vrf_elect(&g_ctx, prev_block_hash, out_addr);\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&g_ctx.rwlock);\n\n    return rc;\n}\n\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- *\n *                        Internal helper functions                          *\n * ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/*\n * ensure_capacity()\n * -----------------\n * Grow the validator array if necessary.\n */\nstatic int\nensure_capacity(pos_ctx_t *ctx)\n{\n    if (ctx->v_len < ctx->v_cap)\n        return 0;\n\n    size_t new_cap = ctx->v_cap * 2;\n    validator_entry_t *tmp = realloc(ctx->validators,\n                                     new_cap * sizeof(validator_entry_t));\n    if (!tmp) {\n        perror(\"[PoS] realloc validators\");\n        return -1;\n    }\n    ctx->validators = tmp;\n    ctx->v_cap = new_cap;\n    return 0;\n}\n\n\n/*\n * find_validator()\n * ----------------\n * Return the index of a validator in the array, or \u20111 if not present.\n * Linear search is acceptable for few hundred validators; for larger sets an\n * ordered map should be used (omitted for brevity).\n */\nstatic ssize_t\nfind_validator(pos_ctx_t *ctx, const wallet_addr_t addr)\n{\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < ctx->v_len; ++i) {\n        if (memcmp(ctx->validators[i].address, addr, WALLET_ADDR_LEN) == 0)\n            return (ssize_t)i;\n    }\n    return -1;\n}\n\n\n/*\n * add_validator()\n * ---------------\n * Append a new validator to the table.\n */\nstatic int\nadd_validator(pos_ctx_t *ctx,\n              const wallet_addr_t addr,\n              uint64_t stake)\n{\n    if (ensure_capacity(ctx) != 0)\n        return -1;\n\n    validator_entry_t *v = &ctx->validators[ctx->v_len++];\n    memset(v, 0, sizeof(*v));\n    memcpy(v->address, addr, WALLET_ADDR_LEN);\n    v->stake        = stake;\n    v->locked_until = ctx->current_epoch + POS_MIN_LOCK_EPOCHS;\n    v->jailed       = false;\n\n    HC_LOG_INFO(\"[PoS] new validator %.8s\u2026, stake=%\" PRIu64,\n                addr, stake);\n    return 0;\n}\n\n\n/*\n * vrf_elect()\n * -----------\n * Perform stake-weighted random election using libsodium's crypto_core_ed25519.\n * The VRF simulates a beacon: H = Hash(prev_hash || validator_pub || epoch).\n * Each validator computes H and compares it with a threshold derived from\n * stake/total.  The smallest valid H wins.  For centralised selection (this\n * service) we compute H for all candidates.\n */\nstatic int\nvrf_elect(const pos_ctx_t *ctx,\n          const uint8_t prev_block_hash[crypto_hash_sha256_BYTES],\n          wallet_addr_t out_selected)\n{\n    uint8_t min_hash[crypto_hash_sha256_BYTES];\n    bool    selected = false;\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < ctx->v_len; ++i) {\n        const validator_entry_t *v = &ctx->validators[i];\n        if (v->jailed || v->stake == 0)\n            continue;\n\n        /* Beacon: hash(prev_hash | validator_pub | epoch_le) */\n        uint8_t buf[crypto_hash_sha256_BYTES + WALLET_ADDR_LEN + sizeof(uint64_t)];\n        size_t  off = 0;\n        memcpy(buf + off, prev_block_hash, crypto_hash_sha256_BYTES); off += crypto_hash_sha256_BYTES;\n        memcpy(buf + off, v->address, WALLET_ADDR_LEN);               off += WALLET_ADDR_LEN;\n        uint64_t epoch_le = htole64(ctx->current_epoch);\n        memcpy(buf + off, &epoch_le, sizeof(epoch_le));\n\n        uint8_t h[crypto_hash_sha256_BYTES];\n        crypto_hash_sha256(h, buf, sizeof(buf));\n\n        /* Convert leading 16 bytes to a 128-bit integer for comparison */\n        if (!selected || memcmp(h, min_hash, 16) < 0) {\n            memcpy(min_hash, h, sizeof(min_hash));\n            memcpy(out_selected, v->address, WALLET_ADDR_LEN);\n            selected = true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (!selected)\n        return -1;\n\n    return 0;\n}\n\n\n/*\n * apply_block_rewards()\n * ---------------------\n * Credit proposer with block reward plus fees, and distribute a portion to\n * delegators (omitted for brevity).\n */\nstatic int\napply_block_rewards(pos_ctx_t *ctx,\n                    const wallet_addr_t proposer,\n                    uint64_t block_fees)\n{\n    static const uint64_t BASE_REWARD = 5 * HC_COINS; /* 5 tokens per block */\n\n    pthread_rwlock_wrlock(&ctx->rwlock);\n    ssize_t idx = find_validator(ctx, proposer);\n    if (idx < 0) {\n        pthread_rwlock_unlock(&ctx->rwlock);\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    validator_entry_t *v = &ctx->validators[idx];\n    v->rewards += BASE_REWARD + block_fees;\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&ctx->rwlock);\n\n    /* Emit reward event */\n    reward_event_t rev = {\n        .validator = {0},\n        .amount    = BASE_REWARD + block_fees\n    };\n    memcpy(rev.validator, proposer, WALLET_ADDR_LEN);\n    event_t ev = {\n        .type    = EVENT_REWARD,\n        .payload = &rev\n    };\n    event_bus_publish(ctx->bus, &ev);\n\n    HC_LOG_DEBUG(\"[PoS] rewarded %.8s\u2026 with %\" PRIu64,\n                 proposer, rev.amount);\n    return 0;\n}\n\n\n/*\n * slash_validator()\n * -----------------\n * Slash a validator for misbehaviour by burning a percentage of its stake and\n * jailing it for several epochs.\n */\nstatic int\nslash_validator(pos_ctx_t *ctx,\n                const wallet_addr_t address,\n                const char *reason)\n{\n    pthread_rwlock_wrlock(&ctx->rwlock);\n    ssize_t idx = find_validator(ctx, address);\n    if (idx < 0) {\n        pthread_rwlock_unlock(&ctx->rwlock);\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    validator_entry_t *v = &ctx->validators[idx];\n    uint64_t penalty = v->stake / POS_SLASH_FRACTION;\n    v->stake -= penalty;\n    v->jailed = true;\n\n    ctx->total_stake -= penalty;\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&ctx->rwlock);\n\n    HC_LOG_WARN(\"[PoS] validator %.8s\u2026 slashed by %\" PRIu64 \" (%s)\",\n                address, penalty, reason);\n\n    /* Emit slashing event */\n    slash_event_t sev = {\n        .validator = {0},\n        .amount    = penalty,\n        .reason    = {0}\n    };\n    memcpy(sev.validator, address, WALLET_ADDR_LEN);\n    strncpy(sev.reason, reason, sizeof(sev.reason)-1);\n\n    event_t ev = {\n        .type    = EVENT_SLASH,\n        .payload = &sev\n    };\n    event_bus_publish(ctx->bus, &ev);\n\n    return 0;\n}\n",

    "content": "/*\n * recipe_composer.c\n *\n * HoloCanvas \u2013 Mint-Factory Microservice\n * --------------------------------------\n * Creates an immutable \u201ccreative recipe\u201d for a to-be-minted artifact by\n * composing user-submitted fragments (GLSL shader code, audio buffers,\n * arbitrary metadata) into a canonical JSON document. The finalized recipe\n * is hashed (SHA-256) and persisted to durable storage (e.g. roll-up chain,\n * IPFS, Cold-DB) while an event is emitted to the mesh for downstream\n * consumers (LedgerCore, Gallery-Gateway, etc.).\n *\n * This module focuses on the composition, hashing, validation, persistence\n * (filesystem-backed for now), and event-publication stubs.\n *\n * Dependencies:\n *   \u2013 OpenSSL libcrypto (SHA-256)\n *   \u2013 cJSON             (JSON construction)\n *   \u2013 librdkafka        (Kafka producer)       [compile-time option]\n *\n * Compile example:\n *   gcc -Wall -Wextra -O2 \\\n *       -DUSE_KAFKA \\\n *       recipe_composer.c -lcjson -lcrypto -lpthread -lrdkafka -o recipe_composer\n *\n * Author:  HoloCanvas Core Team\n */\n\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <stdarg.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include <time.h>\n#include <errno.h>\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <sys/stat.h>\n\n#include <openssl/sha.h>\n#include <cjson/cJSON.h>\n\n#ifdef USE_KAFKA\n#include <rdkafka.h>\n#endif\n\n/* ---------- Constants & Macros ------------------------------------------ */\n\n#define RC_OK                   (0)\n#define RC_ERR_GENERIC          (-1)\n#define RC_ERR_OOM              (-2)\n#define RC_ERR_INVALID_ARG      (-3)\n#define RC_ERR_IO               (-4)\n#define RC_ERR_JSON             (-5)\n#define RC_ERR_STATE            (-6)\n\n#define UNUSED(x)               (void)(x)\n\n#define SHA256_HEX_LENGTH       (SHA256_DIGEST_LENGTH * 2)\n\n/* ---------- Typedefs ---------------------------------------------------- */\n\ntypedef enum {\n    FRAG_SHADER,\n    FRAG_AUDIO,\n    FRAG_METADATA,\n    FRAG_UNKNOWN\n} fragment_type_e;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    fragment_type_e   type;\n    char             *id;        /* user-supplied fragment ID */\n    char             *content;   /* raw content */\n    size_t            content_sz;\n} recipe_fragment_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    char               *artifact_id;\n    char               *author_wallet;\n    recipe_fragment_t **fragments;\n    size_t              frag_count;\n    size_t              frag_capacity;\n    pthread_mutex_t     lock;\n    bool                finalized;\n    char                sha256_hex[SHA256_HEX_LENGTH + 1]; /* null-terminated */\n} recipe_composer_t;\n\n/* ---------- Forward Declarations --------------------------------------- */\n\nstatic int  rc_log_err(int rc, const char *fmt, ...);\nstatic void rc_free_fragment(recipe_fragment_t *frag);\nstatic int  rc_expand_frag_array(recipe_composer_t *rc);\n\n/* ---------- Public API -------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/*\n * rc_create()\n * Initializes a new recipe composer context.\n */\nrecipe_composer_t *\nrc_create(const char *artifact_id, const char *author_wallet)\n{\n    if (!artifact_id || !author_wallet) {\n        rc_log_err(RC_ERR_INVALID_ARG, \"artifact_id and author_wallet required\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    recipe_composer_t *rc = calloc(1, sizeof(*rc));\n    if (!rc) {\n        rc_log_err(RC_ERR_OOM, \"calloc failed\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    rc->artifact_id   = strdup(artifact_id);\n    rc->author_wallet = strdup(author_wallet);\n    rc->frag_capacity = 8; /* start with modest capacity */\n    rc->fragments     = calloc(rc->frag_capacity, sizeof(recipe_fragment_t *));\n    if (!rc->artifact_id || !rc->author_wallet || !rc->fragments) {\n        rc_log_err(RC_ERR_OOM, \"calloc/strdup failed\");\n        free(rc->artifact_id);\n        free(rc->author_wallet);\n        free(rc->fragments);\n        free(rc);\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    pthread_mutex_init(&rc->lock, NULL);\n    return rc;\n}\n\n/*\n * rc_destroy()\n * Frees all resources associated with the composer.\n */\nvoid\nrc_destroy(recipe_composer_t *rc)\n{\n    if (!rc) return;\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < rc->frag_count; ++i)\n        rc_free_fragment(rc->fragments[i]);\n\n    free(rc->fragments);\n    free(rc->artifact_id);\n    free(rc->author_wallet);\n    pthread_mutex_destroy(&rc->lock);\n    free(rc);\n}\n\n/*\n * rc_add_fragment()\n * Adds a fragment to the recipe. Ownership of `content` is transferred to the\n * composer on success (caller must malloc it).\n */\nint\nrc_add_fragment(recipe_composer_t *rc,\n                fragment_type_e type,\n                const char     *fragment_id,\n                char           *content,\n                size_t          content_sz)\n{\n    if (!rc || !fragment_id || !content || content_sz == 0)\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_INVALID_ARG,\n                          \"add_fragment() invalid arguments\");\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&rc->lock);\n\n    if (rc->finalized) {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_STATE,\n                          \"cannot add fragment: recipe already finalized\");\n    }\n\n    /* Capacity expansion if needed */\n    if (rc->frag_count >= rc->frag_capacity &&\n        rc_expand_frag_array(rc) != RC_OK) {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_OOM, \"expanding fragment array failed\");\n    }\n\n    recipe_fragment_t *frag = calloc(1, sizeof(*frag));\n    if (!frag) {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_OOM, \"calloc failed\");\n    }\n    frag->type       = type;\n    frag->id         = strdup(fragment_id);\n    frag->content    = content;       /* take ownership */\n    frag->content_sz = content_sz;\n\n    if (!frag->id) {\n        rc_free_fragment(frag);\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_OOM, \"strdup failed\");\n    }\n\n    rc->fragments[rc->frag_count++] = frag;\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n    return RC_OK;\n}\n\n/*\n * rc_finalize()\n * Assembles JSON, computes SHA-256, persists to disk, and emits Kafka event.\n */\nint\nrc_finalize(recipe_composer_t *rc,\n            const char *storage_path,   /* directory for recipe JSON */\n            const char *kafka_topic)    /* optional, NULL to skip */\n{\n    if (!rc || !storage_path)\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_INVALID_ARG, \"finalize() invalid arguments\");\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&rc->lock);\n    if (rc->finalized) {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_STATE, \"recipe already finalized\");\n    }\n\n    /* -------------------- Build JSON -------------------- */\n    cJSON *root = cJSON_CreateObject();\n    if (!root) {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_JSON, \"failed to create JSON root\");\n    }\n\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(root, \"artifact_id\", rc->artifact_id);\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(root, \"author_wallet\", rc->author_wallet);\n\n    char iso8601[32] = {0};\n    time_t now = time(NULL);\n    strftime(iso8601, sizeof iso8601, \"%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ\", gmtime(&now));\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(root, \"timestamp\", iso8601);\n\n    cJSON *frag_arr = cJSON_AddArrayToObject(root, \"fragments\");\n    if (!frag_arr) {\n        cJSON_Delete(root);\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_JSON, \"failed to create JSON array\");\n    }\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < rc->frag_count; ++i) {\n        recipe_fragment_t *f = rc->fragments[i];\n        cJSON *entry = cJSON_CreateObject();\n        cJSON_AddStringToObject(entry, \"id\", f->id);\n\n        switch (f->type) {\n            case FRAG_SHADER:   cJSON_AddStringToObject(entry, \"type\", \"shader\");   break;\n            case FRAG_AUDIO:    cJSON_AddStringToObject(entry, \"type\", \"audio\");    break;\n            case FRAG_METADATA: cJSON_AddStringToObject(entry, \"type\", \"metadata\"); break;\n            default:            cJSON_AddStringToObject(entry, \"type\", \"unknown\");  break;\n        }\n        /* Content is stored as base64 to keep JSON/text-safe */\n        char *b64 = NULL;\n        size_t b64_len = 0;\n        {\n            /* --- simplistic Base64 encoding using OpenSSL BIO --- */\n            BIO *bio, *b64f;\n            BUF_MEM *buffer_ptr = NULL;\n\n            b64f = BIO_new(BIO_f_base64());\n            bio  = BIO_new(BIO_s_mem());\n            b64f = BIO_push(b64f, bio);\n\n            BIO_set_flags(b64f, BIO_FLAGS_BASE64_NO_NL);\n            BIO_write(b64f, f->content, (int)f->content_sz);\n            BIO_flush(b64f);\n            BIO_get_mem_ptr(b64f, &buffer_ptr);\n\n            b64 = malloc(buffer_ptr->length + 1);\n            if (b64) {\n                memcpy(b64, buffer_ptr->data, buffer_ptr->length);\n                b64[buffer_ptr->length] = 0;\n                b64_len = buffer_ptr->length;\n            }\n            BIO_free_all(b64f);\n        }\n\n        if (!b64) {\n            cJSON_Delete(root);\n            pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n            return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_OOM, \"base64 encoding failed\");\n        }\n\n        cJSON_AddStringToObject(entry, \"content_b64\", b64);\n        free(b64);\n        cJSON_AddItemToArray(frag_arr, entry);\n    }\n\n    char *json_text = cJSON_PrintUnformatted(root);\n    cJSON_Delete(root);\n    if (!json_text) {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_JSON, \"cJSON_Print failed\");\n    }\n\n    /* -------------------- Compute SHA-256 -------------------- */\n    unsigned char digest[SHA256_DIGEST_LENGTH];\n    SHA256((unsigned char *)json_text, strlen(json_text), digest);\n\n    for (int i = 0; i < SHA256_DIGEST_LENGTH; ++i)\n        sprintf(rc->sha256_hex + (i * 2), \"%02x\", digest[i]);\n\n    /* -------------------- Persist to storage -------------------- */\n    if (mkdir(storage_path, 0755) != 0 && errno != EEXIST) {\n        free(json_text);\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_IO, \"mkdir '%s' failed: %s\",\n                          storage_path, strerror(errno));\n    }\n\n    char file_path[1024];\n    snprintf(file_path, sizeof file_path, \"%s/%s.json\", storage_path,\n             rc->sha256_hex);\n\n    FILE *fp = fopen(file_path, \"w\");\n    if (!fp) {\n        free(json_text);\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_IO, \"fopen '%s' failed: %s\",\n                          file_path, strerror(errno));\n    }\n\n    if (fwrite(json_text, 1, strlen(json_text), fp)\n        != strlen(json_text)) {\n        fclose(fp);\n        unlink(file_path);\n        free(json_text);\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n        return rc_log_err(RC_ERR_IO, \"fwrite failed\");\n    }\n    fclose(fp);\n\n    /* -------------------- Emit event -------------------- */\n#ifdef USE_KAFKA\n    if (kafka_topic) {\n        char errstr[512];\n        rd_kafka_conf_t *conf = rd_kafka_conf_new();\n        rd_kafka_conf_set(conf, \"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\",\n                          errstr, sizeof errstr);\n\n        rd_kafka_t *rk = rd_kafka_new(RD_KAFKA_PRODUCER, conf,\n                                      errstr, sizeof errstr);\n        if (!rk) {\n            rc_log_err(RC_ERR_GENERIC, \"rd_kafka_new failed: %s\", errstr);\n        } else {\n            rd_kafka_resp_err_t rerr;\n            rerr = rd_kafka_producev(\n                rk,\n                RD_KAFKA_V_TOPIC(kafka_topic),\n                RD_KAFKA_V_VALUE(rc->sha256_hex, SHA256_HEX_LENGTH),\n                RD_KAFKA_V_END);\n            if (rerr)\n                rc_log_err(RC_ERR_GENERIC, \"kafka produce failed: %s\",\n                           rd_kafka_err2str(rerr));\n\n            rd_kafka_flush(rk, 3000);\n            rd_kafka_destroy(rk);\n        }\n    }\n#else\n    UNUSED(kafka_topic);\n#endif\n\n    /* mark finalized */\n    rc->finalized = true;\n    free(json_text);\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&rc->lock);\n    return RC_OK;\n}\n\n/*\n * rc_get_sha256()\n * Returns the hex-encoded SHA-256 hash after finalize().\n */\nconst char *\nrc_get_sha256(recipe_composer_t *rc)\n{\n    if (!rc || !rc->finalized) return NULL;\n    return rc->sha256_hex;\n}\n\n/* ---------- Internal Helpers ------------------------------------------- */\n\nstatic int\nrc_log_err(int rc, const char *fmt, ...)\n{\n    va_list ap;\n    va_start(ap, fmt);\n    fprintf(stderr, \"[recipe_composer] ERROR: \");\n    vfprintf(stderr, fmt, ap);\n    fprintf(stderr, \"\\n\");\n    va_end(ap);\n    return rc;\n}\n\nstatic void\nrc_free_fragment(recipe_fragment_t *frag)\n{\n    if (!frag) return;\n    free(frag->id);\n    free(frag->content);\n    free(frag);\n}\n\nstatic int\nrc_expand_frag_array(recipe_composer_t *rc)\n{\n    size_t new_cap = rc->frag_capacity * 2;\n    recipe_fragment_t **tmp =\n        realloc(rc->fragments, new_cap * sizeof(recipe_fragment_t *));\n    if (!tmp) return RC_ERR_OOM;\n    rc->fragments = tmp;\n    rc->frag_capacity = new_cap;\n    return RC_OK;\n}\n\n/* ---------- Test Harness (optional) ------------------------------------ */\n#ifdef RC_UNIT_TEST\n\nstatic char rc_get_sha256(rc));\n    rc_destroy(rc);\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n\nstatic char *\nslurp_file(const char *path, size_t *out_sz)\n{\n    FILE *fp = fopen(path, \"rb\");\n    if (!fp) {\n        perror(path);\n        return NULL;\n    }\n    fseek(fp, 0, SEEK_END);\n    long len = ftell(fp);\n    rewind(fp);\n\n    char *buf = malloc(len);\n    if (!buf) { fclose(fp); return NULL; }\n\n buf;\n}\n\n#endif /* RC_UNIT_TEST */\n",

  "content": "# HoloCanvas Architectural Bottleneck Analysis for NFT Minting Throughput\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis document presents a comprehensive architectural analysis of the HoloCanvas NFT minting system, identifies the primary performance bottleneck causing latency during peak load, and proposes a high-level architectural modification to improve throughput.\n\n---\n\n## 1. End-to-End Minting Data Flow Analysis\n\n### 1.1 Overview\n\nHoloCanvas is a C-based microservice ecosystem that orchestrates the minting, governance, and market evolution of generative NFTs. The services communicate through **Kafka** event streams and **gRPC** contracts, as documented in `ARCHITECTURE.md:27-28`.\n\n### 1.2 Complete Minting Lifecycle\n\nThe minting flow traverses the following services:\n\n```\nUser \u2192 Wallet-Proxy \u2192 LedgerCore \u2192 Consensus \u2192 Mint-Factory \u2192 Gallery-Gateway\n```\n\n#### Step 1: User Request Entry (Wallet-Proxy)\n\n**File:** `services/wallet_proxy/src/proxy_server.c`\n\nThe user initiates a mint request through the Wallet-Proxy, which provides:\n- Wallet creation using Ed25519 key pairs (`proxy_server.c:258-290`)\n- Transaction signing (`proxy_server.c:332-400`)\n- Transaction broadcast to LedgerCore (`proxy_server.c:402-443`)\n\nThe `handle_tx_broadcast()` function at line 402 calls `ledger_broadcast_transaction()` to forward signed transactions to LedgerCore.\n\n#### Step 2: Transaction Processing (LedgerCore)\n\n**Files:**\n- `services/ledger_core/src/transaction_processor.c`\n- `services/ledger_core/src/block_builder.c`\n- `services/ledger_core/src/consensus_manager.c`\n\n**Transaction Processor (`transaction_processor.c:147-200`):**\n\nThe `tp_process()` function handles incoming transactions through a synchronous validation pipeline:\n1. **Decode** - Deserializes the transaction (`tx_decode()`)\n2. **Signature Verification** - Ed25519 signature verification (`tp_verify_signature()` at line 209-232)\n3. **Nonce Verification** - Anti-replay protection (`tp_verify_nonce()` at line 238-252)\n4. **Funds Verification** - Balance validation (`tp_verify_funds()` at line 257-275)\n5. **State Application** - Mutates ledger state under a **global mutex** (`tp_apply()` at line 288-352)\n\nCritical observation from `transaction_processor.c:286-287`:\n```c\n/* NOTE: called inside the global mutex for now. In production deployments\n   we may employ sharded, fine-grained locks or MVCC to improve throughput. */\n```\n\n**Block Builder (`block_builder.c:147-222`):**\n\nThe block builder runs in a dedicated worker thread that:\n1. Monitors the mempool for pending transactions\n2. Triggers block creation based on:\n   - Transaction count threshold (`cfg.max_txs_per_block`)\n   - Time-based interval (`cfg.max_block_interval_ms`)\n3. Builds a Merkle tree of transactions (`compute_merkle_root()` at line 279-322)\n4. Submits candidate blocks to the consensus engine (`consensus_submit_block()` at line 204)\n\n**Consensus Manager (`consensus_manager.c:297-357`):**\n\nThe consensus manager's worker loop (`_worker_loop()`) processes blocks **sequentially**:\n1. Dequeues a candidate block (`_dequeue_block()`)\n2. **Verifies** the block via pluggable consensus engine (`engine.verify_block()` at line 308)\n3. **Finalizes** state transitions (`engine.finalise_block()` at line 320)\n4. **Commits** to durable storage (`ledger_storage_put_block()` at line 333)\n5. **Publishes** \"ledger.block.finalised\" event to Kafka (`event_bus_publish()` at line 344)\n\n#### Step 3: Consensus Engine (PoS Strategy)\n\n**File:** `services/ledger_core/src/strategies/pos_strategy.c`\n\nThe Proof-of-Stake consensus plugin (`pos_strategy.c`) performs:\n- Validator selection via VRF (`vrf_elect()` at line 427-463)\n- Block verification (`crypto_verify_block()`)\n- Reward distribution (`apply_block_rewards()` at line 472-505)\n\nThe `pos_strategy_handle_block()` function (line 273-312) validates blocks synchronously, verifying signatures and proposer eligibility **for each block**.\n\n#### Step 4: Event Propagation to Mint-Factory\n\n**File:** `services/mint_factory/src/event_handler.c`\n\nThe Mint-Factory's event handler subscribes to Kafka topics and consumes events in a dedicated thread (`run_loop()` at line 201-248):\n- Parses incoming JSON events (`parse_event()` at line 262-319)\n- Dispatches to appropriate handlers based on event type:\n  - `EVT_MINT_REQUEST` \u2192 `mint_engine_handle_request()` (line 340)\n  - `EVT_BID` \u2192 `mint_engine_handle_bid()` (line 345)\n\n**Key Configuration from `event_handler.c:55-60`:**\n```c\n#define KAFKA_TOPICS \"mint-factory.events\"\n#define KAFKA_CONSUMER_POLL_TIMEOUT_MS 250\n```\n\n#### Step 5: Artifact Generation (Mint-Factory)\n\n**Files:**\n- `services/mint_factory/src/recipe_composer.c`\n- `services/mint_factory/src/artifact_factory.c`\n\n**Recipe Composer (`recipe_composer.c`):**\n- Assembles creative fragments (shader, audio, metadata) into canonical JSON\n- Computes SHA-256 hash for deterministic artifact ID\n- **Synchronously persists** to disk and optionally emits Kafka event\n\n**Artifact Factory (`artifact_factory.c:176-252`):**\n\nThe `af_mint()` function performs:\n1. Fragment validation (`validate_fragments()`)\n2. JSON recipe composition (`compose_recipe_json()`)\n3. SHA-256 ID generation (`sha256_hex()`)\n4. **Synchronous persistence** to LedgerCore (`persist_to_ledger()` at line 219)\n5. Event emission (\"ArtifactMinted\" to `artifact.events` topic at line 238)\n\n#### Step 6: Gallery Update (Gallery-Gateway)\n\n**File:** `services/gallery_gateway/src/query_service.c`\n\nThe query service maintains an LRU cache and federates data from LedgerCore:\n- `gallery_query_get_artifact()` (line 459-510) retrieves artifact state\n- Cache TTL: 5 minutes (`DEFAULT_CACHE_TTL_SEC` at line 52)\n- Falls back to HTTP GET from LedgerCore endpoint\n\n### 1.3 Kafka Topic Configuration\n\n**File:** `config/kafka_topics.json`\n\nKey topics in the minting flow:\n| Topic | Purpose | Partitions |\n|-------|---------|------------|\n| `ledgercore.tx.incoming` | Raw transactions to LedgerCore | 9 |\n| `mint-factory.request` | Minting requests | 12 |\n| `mint-factory.artifact.minted` | Successful mint notifications | 3 |\n| `consensus.block.finalized` | Block finalization events | 3 |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Architectural Bottleneck Identification\n\n### 2.1 Primary Bottleneck: Serial Block Processing in LedgerCore Consensus\n\nThe **primary scalability bottleneck** is the **serial, synchronous block processing** in the LedgerCore consensus layer.\n\n#### Evidence:\n\n**1. Single-threaded Consensus Worker (`consensus_manager.c:297-357`):**\n\n```c\nstatic void *_worker_loop(void *arg)\n{\n    consensus_manager_t *mgr = arg;\n    for (;;) {\n        block_t *blk = _dequeue_block(mgr);  // BLOCKING dequeue\n        if (!blk) break;\n\n        // Step 1: Verify candidate block - SYNCHRONOUS\n        if (!mgr->engine.verify_block(blk, &err_msg)) { ... }\n\n        // Step 2: Finalise - SYNCHRONOUS\n        if (!mgr->engine.finalise_block(blk, new_state_root, &err_msg)) { ... }\n\n        // Step 3: Commit to storage - SYNCHRONOUS\n        if (!ledger_storage_put_block(mgr->storage, blk) || ...) { ... }\n\n        // Step 4: Publish event - only AFTER all above complete\n        event_bus_publish(mgr->event_bus, \"ledger.block.finalised\", blk, sizeof(*blk));\n    }\n}\n```\n\nBlocks are processed **one at a time**, serially. Each block must be fully verified, finalized, and committed before the next block can be processed.\n\n**2. Global Mutex in Transaction Processor (`transaction_processor.c:286-352`):**\n\n```c\nstatic int tp_apply(txp_ctx_t *ctx, const tx_t *tx, uint64_t ts_unix)\n{\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&ctx->mtx);  // GLOBAL LOCK\n\n    /* All ledger mutations happen here under a single lock */\n    ledger_append(ctx->ledger, &entry);\n    ledger_inc_nonce(ctx->ledger, tx->from);\n    ledger_debit(ctx->ledger, tx->from, ...);\n    ledger_credit(ctx->ledger, tx->to, tx->value);\n\n    /* Domain-specific mutations also serialized */\n    switch (tx->type) {\n        case TX_MINT_NFT:\n            artifact_state_on_mint(ctx->ledger, &tx->payload.mint);\n            break;\n        // ...\n    }\n\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&ctx->mtx);\n}\n```\n\nThe code explicitly acknowledges this limitation in the comment: *\"In production deployments we may employ sharded, fine-grained locks or MVCC to improve throughput.\"*\n\n**3. Per-Block Consensus Overhead (`pos_strategy.c:273-312`):**\n\nEach block requires:\n- Cryptographic signature verification (`crypto_verify_block()`)\n- Validator lookup and state validation\n- VRF-based proposer selection for the next block\n- Reward distribution calculations\n\n**4. Sequential Kafka Event Publishing:**\n\nThe `ledger.block.finalised` event is only published **after** all synchronous operations complete. Downstream services (Mint-Factory, Gallery-Gateway) cannot proceed until this event arrives.\n\n### 2.2 Secondary Bottleneck: Synchronous Artifact Generation\n\nThe Mint-Factory's artifact generation is also synchronous:\n\n**`artifact_factory.c:218-224`:**\n```c\n/* Persist recipe to LedgerCore */\nif (!persist_to_ledger(artifact_id, recipe_str))\n{\n    HC_LOG_ERROR(\"artifact_factory: failed to persist artifact to ledger\");\n    free(recipe_str);\n    return AF_STATUS_ERR_DEPENDENCY;\n}\n```\n\nThis creates a **synchronous round-trip** back to LedgerCore for each mint, compounding the consensus bottleneck.\n\n### 2.3 Impact During Peak Load\n\nDuring \"evolution events\" triggered by Muse-Observer:\n1. A surge of mint requests floods `ledgercore.tx.incoming`\n2. Transactions queue in the mempool waiting for block inclusion\n3. Block builder creates candidate blocks\n4. Consensus processes blocks **one at a time**\n5. Each block finalization creates backpressure\n6. Mint-Factory waits for block finalization events\n7. Gallery-Gateway waits for artifact creation events\n8. Users experience minutes of latency instead of seconds\n\n---\n\n## 3. Proposed Architectural Solution: Batch Aggregation with Off-Chain Pre-Commitment\n\n### 3.1 High-Level Design\n\nTransform the one-by-one transaction model into a **batch aggregation** architecture using an off-chain pre-commitment queue.\n\n```\n                     \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n                     \u2502     NEW: Batch Aggregator Service   \u2502\n                     \u2502  (Aggregates mint intents off-chain)\u2502\n                     \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n
